GA-YENG BA'I TSE LO BRGYA BRGYA

SBAR GANG GTOR NA DER CHAGS PA

CUNG ZAD 'THUD NUS PA YIN, SEMS GNAS 'DI GNYIS LA BYING RGOD
CHES MANG ZHING TING 'DZIN NYUNG DU LAS MI 'ONG BAS YID BYED
BZHI'I NANG GI DANG PO BSGRIMS TE 'JUG

PA'I SKABS SO,, DE NAS CUNG ZAD GOMS PA NA LUNG PA PHU GSUM GYI
RDZING CHU LTA BU 'GAL RKYEN GYIS MANG DKRUGS PA'I TSE SEMS GNAS
BA SNYAM BYED LA, RKYEN BYUNG TSE MI GNAS PA'I RNAM RTOG THANG
CHAD PA'I NYAMS SHIG 'ONG, DE'I TSE STOBS

GSUM PA DRAN PAS 'GRUB PA'I SEMS GNAS GSUM BA GLAN TE 'JOG PA
ZHES BYA BA SEMS GA-YENG BA MYUR DU RTOGS NAS SLAR DMIGS PA LA
GLON PA DANG, SEMS GNAS BZHI PA NYE BAR 'JOG PA ZHES BYA BA RGYA
CHEN PO LAS BSDUS TE

@077A *, ,PHRA BAR BYED PA DANG, STOBS BZHI PA SHES BZHIN GYIS
'GRUB PA'I SEMS GNAS LNGA PA DUL BAR BYED PA ZHES BYA BA TING
NGE 'DZIN GYI YON TAN LA DGA' BA DANG, SEMS GNAS DRUG PA ZHI BAR
BYED PA ZHES BYA BA RNAMS

GA-YENG GI NYES DMIGS RIG NAS 'GOG PA DANG, STOBS LNGA PA BRTZON
'GRUS KYIS 'GRUB PA'I SEMS GNAS LA BDUN PA DANG BRGYAD PA GNYIS
YOD PA'I BDUN BA RNAM PAR ZHI BAR BYED PA ZHES BYA BA CHAGS SEMS
NYON MONGS RTZOL

BAS SPANGS TE ZHI BAR BYED, SEMS GNAS GSUM BA NAS BDUN PA'I BAR
GYI LNGA PO 'DI LA BYING RGOD KYIS BAR DU GCOD PAS YID BYED
BZHI'I NANG GI GNYIS BA SKABS SU CHAD CING 'JUG PA'I DUS SO, ,DE
NAS RIM GYIS BSGOMS

BAS RGYA MTSO RLABS DANG BCAS PA LTA BU RNAM RTOG CI BYUNG YANG
GNYEN PO DRAN 'DZIN CUNG ZAD BSTEN PAS RANG MA LA DU ZHI'I 'GRO
BAS RNAM RTOG 'DU BYED PA ZHES BYA BA'I NYAMS 'ONG, DE'I TSE
SNGAR BSHAD PA'I STOBS LNGA PAS 'GRUB PA'I

SEMS GNAS BRGYAD PA RTZE GCIG TU BYED PA ZHES BYA BA TING NGE
'DZIN RGYUN CHAGS SU 'GRUB PA YIN NO, ,SEMS GNAS BRGYAD PA LA
BYING RGOD KYiS BAR DU MI GCOD BAR YID BYED BZHI'I NANG GI GSUM
BA SKABS SU CHAD PA MED

PAR 'JUG PA'I DUS SO, ,DE NAS RIM GYIS BSGOMS PAS RGYA MTSO
RLABS DANG BRAL BA LTA BU YUL RKYAN CI BYUNG YANG GNYEN PO DRAN
'DZIN GYI 'BAD RTZOL LA MA BLTOS PAR TING 'DZIN RANG BABS SU
'CHAR BAS RNAM RTOG MNGON PAR

'DU MI BYED PA'I NYAMS KYI MNYAM GZHAG 'ONG, ,DE'I TSE STOBS
DRUG PA YONGS SU 'DRIS PA LAS 'GRUB PA'I SEMS GNAS DGU PA MNYAM
PAR 'JOG BA ZHES BYA BA RTZOL MED DU DMIGS PA LA 'JOG PAS YID
BYED BZHI'I NANG GI BZHI BA LHUN

@077B GYIS GRUB PAR 'JUG PA'I DUS SO, ,'DI'I SKABS SU BYING
RGOD 'GOG PA'I RTZOL BA SKYON DU 'GYUR BAR DGONGS NAS GONG MA

'DI DAG LEGS PAR SHES DGOS KYI, PUS 'KHYUD SGOM ZHVA DRA PAD

'JUG PA DANG BAR PA LNGA LA CHAD

BAR BAR LA BYING RGOD KYIS YANG YANG GCOD

,THUB GSUNG MES PO'I ZHAL SGO LAS BABS PA'I, ,BKA' DANG DGONGS
'GREL YAN LAG BRGYAD

LDAN CHAB, ,BTUNGS PAS DRANG NGES 'BYED MKHAS BTZONG KHA PA,
,BSNGON MED RDZHA NU ZHES KUN GNYIS GLENG, ,GANG GI RING LUGS
'DZIN 'DOD KUN BZOD 'DIR, ,CHES MANG LCI BA'I RDUL GYI 'BAB
LDAN MAS, ,NOR 'DZIN BZHIN RAS YONGS SU BKRUS

BYAS KYANG, ,TSUL LDAN SHES PA'I MKHAS PA NYIN SKAR BZHIN,
,'CHAD RTZOD RTZOM LA SPOBS PA'I MGRIN MTHON PO, ,MA SMAD
GA-YAS SU 'KHYIL BA'I CHOS KYI DUNG, ,SKAL BZANG RNA BAR SGROG
PA'I YONGS 'DZIN TSOGS, ,THAMS CAD MKHYEN

PAR NGES SO GZHAN LAS CI, ,PHYOGS RE'I SMAN GYIS LA LA'I DUG
'GYUR BA'I, ,ZAB RLOM GZHAN GYIS 'GRAN MIN BSTAN PA'I GNAD,
,MA LUS TSANG BAS SKYES BU RNAMS PAR GSUM, ,YANG DAG LAM DU
BKRI BA'I DON CHEN YIN, ,LAM

@093A *, ,RIM GNYIS KYI TSIG DON ZAB BRLING MKHA', ,BLO GROS
CHUNG DU'I BUG PAR SHOD MIN LA, ,PHAN 'DOD GSAR BSKRUN MTHA'
GNYIS LHUNG BA'I CHU, ,DBANG PO'I SNOD DU MI KHENGS LA LAR
'BO, ,YANG DAG DON GYI 'BRAS BU SMIN

PA LA, ,GNAD 'GAG MTSANG SKAM PO'I YAL GA DANG, ,DON MED TSIG
GI LO MA'I PHANG PHUNG YANG, ,RI MO'I MAR ME JI BZHIN GSAL
CHAS STONG, ,DE PHYIR DON GYI CHA SHAS KUN TSANG ZHING, ,RGYA
CHEN TSIG GI RI DVAGS GZUGS BRAL BA'I, ,SNGON

MED BSTAN BCOS ZLA BA GSAR PA 'DI, ,BDAG BLO'I RDZING LAS
SKRUN NUS GA LA SRID, ,'ON TE GZHUNG DON RTOGS DKA'I GNAD KYI
RGYUD, ,MANG THOS SOR MO'I RTZAL GYIS BKUG PA'I MDAS, ,PHRA
ZHIB LEGS BSHAD RGYANG MA'I TSAD BZHAG TSE,,

MKHAS RLOM 'PHONGS SKYEN RNAMS KYI KHENGS PA PHROGS, ,LUNG DON
RIGS PAS DPYOD PA'I PHA MTHA' LA, ,GZIGS PA'I SBYAN GYI DKYUS
DE CHES THUNG YANG, ,MI DGE'I GTAM GYI GAR SGYUR LJAGS KYI
RTZE, ,SRID PA'I RTZE MOR SNYEG RNAMS NGAL

GSO MDZOD, ,GUR KUM TSOS KYIS BTZOS PA'I LA BA'I ZHVAS, ,RANG
RIGS BSTAN PA ZIN NA CHES LEGS KYI, ,PHA MES LUNG DANG RTOGS
PA'I KHYAD NOR TSOGS, ,RNAM GA-YENG RKUN POR SHOR BA'I LAG
STONG MANG, ,GTI MUG GOMS PA'I

DBANG RTUL RA GNA LA, ,BSTAN 'DZIN DAM PA'I GSER SBYANGS BTZO
MA ZHES, ,MKHAS MANG TSONG 'DUS CHEN PO'I SAR 'GRIMS TSE, ,MI

CI, ,KHO BO MA BSLABS MKHYEN PA'I SNYAN GRAGS KYI, ,CAL SGROG
MANG PO'I YID DBANG MA PHROGS KYANG, ,PHONGS

@093B BA'I NOR BZHIN 'BAD PAS BSGRUBS PA YI, ,LNGA RIG PHYOGS
TZAM SHES 'DIS GZENGS SU MTHO, ,MDZAD MCHOG GSUNG GI SNYING PO
DKA' BA'I MDUD, ,RNAM PAR 'GROL BA'I BSOD NAMS SU WARnA'I,
,'KHOR LO RTZIBS STONG 'BAR BAS MI

'JIGS BZHI'I, ,BANG RIM RTZE MO'I KHANG PAR BGROD GYUR CIG
,ZHVA SER MNABS PA'I LUGS 'DZIN SKYONG BA'I LHA, ,PHYAG DRUG
LAS GSHIN LHA CHEN MIG GI MES, ,'DOD LHA SDE BCAS SREG DANG
CHABS CIG PAR, ,LUNG RTOGS BA DAN SRID

RTZER SGRENG GYUR CIG ,RANG BLO'I DROD KYIS 'KHRID GZHUNG GSER
SGONG DAG ,SMIN PA'I 'BRAS BZANG SKU BZHI'I ZHAL SGO CAN, ,MI
ZAD RGYAN GYI 'KHOR LO'I BYED PA PO, ,KUN MKHYEN MES POR 'GRO
RNAMS GYUR CIG GU, DE LTAR BYANG CHUB LAM GYI

RIM PA'I 'KHRID GZHUNG SPYAN SNGA BLO GROS RGYAL MTSAN GYIS
MDZAD PA SOGS 'GA' ZHIG SNANG BA STOD CHA RNAMS BSHAD YAMS SU
SONG PAS DMIGS PA'I THOG TU MI 'DRIL LA, SMAD CHA RNAMS HA
CANG BSDUS BAS GANG ZAG LAS DANG PO

RNAMS LA NYE BAR MI MKHO ZHING, BLO GROS KYI RTZAL DANG LDAN
BA RNAMS NI THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA BTZONG KHA PA CHEN PO'I GSUNG
RAB LA BLTA BA'I BLO GROS KYI MIG DANG LDAN BZHIN DU YI GE
GZHAN LA BRTEN PA YAN LAG BRGYAD LDAN GYI MTSO

'GRAM DU BA TSVA'I KHRON PA'I DPER SONG MOD, BRGYUD BA'I BKA'
SROL 'DI PAR THAMS CAD MKHYEN PA BSOD NAMS RGYA MTSO YAN CHOD
DU LAM RIM GNYIS DANG, BLA MA BRGYUD BA'I ZHAL LUNG NYAMS PA
MED PA NYID LAS ZIN BRIS KYI YI GE

'DI LA BRTEN GYI SGROS MI 'DUG CING, SBYAN SNGA RIN PO CHE
GZHON NU CHOS DPAL BZANG PO YAN CHOD DU BDUD RTZI GSER GYI
YANG ZHUN LA RTZA BAR MDZAD, LAM RIM CHE CHUNG GNYIS NAS KHA
BKANG STE GNANG PA LAS 'KHRID YIG NAG 'GROS

@094A *, ,SU BKOD PA MED KYANG, YUL NYANG STOD DPAL 'KHOR BDE
BA CHEN PO'I SGRUB SDE RI KHROD DGA' LDAN GYI SLOB DPON PA, AE
RIG PA'I 'BYUNG GNAS KYI YUL GRUR SKYES BA'I MDO SNGAGS RAB
'BYAMS SMRA BA BYAMS PA RIN

CHEN GYIS 'BAD PA CHEN POS ZLA BA PHYED GNYIS KYI BAR DU NYAMS
'KHRID SMIN RGYAS SU MNOS TE, 'KHRID DMIGS YI GER 'KHOD PA
ZHIG DGOS ZHES NAN GYIS BSKUL BA LA BRTEN NAS, SPYIR NYAMS
'KHRID KYI RIGS BRGYUD LDAN BLA MA'I

ZHAL SGO LAS NYE BAR MNOS PA ZHIG MA BYUNG NA, KLAG LUNG DANG
